 In the much-publicized Batla House encounter, the Saket court pronounced its verdict, terming the accused Shahzad Ahmed as the culprit in the case and asked to debate his sentence on Monday
 isi faisale ke saath hi is encounter ke farzi hone or naa hone par par chali aa rahi bahes par phulstop lag gaya

 adaalat ne kaha, 'tamaam sabooton or gavaahon ke maddenzar adaalat shahzad ahamed ko taziraat-e-hind kii dafaa 302, 307, 353, 186, 333, 34 or arms act ke tahat gunahagaar maanati he or ab uski sazaa par somvaar ko bahes kii jaaegi
 In the charge sheet filed against Shahzad, the Delhi Police had requested him to prosecute him as a culprit in many other matters besides these sections, on which the police presented many evidence and argued during the hearing, while the defendants Opposed him
 lekin akhirkaar adaalat ne use inspector mohanchand sharma kaa qatl karne, duusare pulisavaalon par jaanaleva hamalaa karne, sarkari kaam main baadha daalane ke iraade se pulisavaalon par hamalaa karne or arms act kii dafaaon ke tahat kusuuravaar paaya
 However, Shahzad's lawyer and his family have expressed unhappiness over the decision, challenging the decision in the High Court
 is encounter ko hi farzi bataate hue bachaav paksh kaa kahana he ki wo shuru se hi is maamle kii nyaayik jaanch kii maang karti rahi he

 After the serial blasts in Delhi, last September 19, 2008, Special Cell raided a flat in Batla House area to catch the terrorists
 is dauraan hue encounter main inspector mohanchand sharma shahid hue the, jabaki kuch pulisavaale zakhmi hue the
 Two terrorists named Sajid and Atif were killed in the encounter, while Shahzad and Junaid managed to escape from the spot
 baad main shahzad ko police ne azamgarh se giraftaar kiya tha, jabaki junayd ab tak police kii giraft main nahin aayaa he
 Shehzad Ahmed is the culprit for the murder of Inspector Mohanchand Sharma
 
 
 dilli ke saket court ne is hakeekat par apni muhar laga di he
 Relief from the verdict has also been given to Delhi Police, which had been living with the burden of suspicion of fake encounter for the last 5 years
 19 sitambar 2008 ke batla house ke makaan number el 18 main hue encounter ko hi farzi bataate hue bachaav paksh kaa kahana he ki vah shuru se hi is maamle kii nyaayik jaanch kii maang karata rahaa he
 Now the wait is July 29, the day when the sentence on Shehzad will be debated
 aatanki shahzad ahamed he koun?shahzad mul rup se uttar pradesh ke azamgarh jile ke khalispur gaanv kaa rahane vaala he
 Shehzad is part of the terrorist organization Indian Mujahideen, which opened fire on Inspector Mohanchand Sharma at the Batla House encounter on 19 September 2008
 encounter ke baad shahzad junayd naam ke aaropee ke saath maukey se faraar ho gaya tha, lekin police ko shahzad kaa passport mil chukaa tha

 shahzad par 13 sitambar 2008 main hue dilli serial blast main shaamil hone kaa bhi aarope he

 ab shahzad kaa parivaar 29 july ke baad court ke sajaa par faisla kaa intjaar kar rahaa he, jiske baad aage kii ranneeti tay karengen
 How is Sanjarpur in Azamgarh related to L-18 of Batla House in Delhi? After all, how did the five boys from Sanjarpur reach L-18 directly from the village? After all, how did the straightforward boys of the village become terrorists? Shahzad Ahmed alias Pappu's hands are stained with blood
 is baat par muhar ab adaalat bhi laga chuki he

 The police investigation is also revealing that Shehzad belongs to the terrorist organization Indian Mujahideen, which has shown horrific pictures of destruction in different parts of the country
 sanjarpur ek chota-sa gaanv he, jisaki aabaadi he mahaj 15 hajaar, par 15 hajaar kii aabaadi vaala yah gaanv hindustan ke nakshe par sabase alag, sabase juda dikhaai detaa he
 Do you know why? Because out of the 18 people who have been held responsible for the blasts in the last few years across the country, 16 boys are from this one village alone
 dilli main 13 sintabar 2008 ko hue dhamaakon or 19 sintabar 2008 ko hue batla house enkanutor ke mahaz haftebhar baad ajtak kii team is gaanv kaa sach jaanane vahaan gai thi
 Sanjarpur village is almost adjacent to Sarai Mir, about thirty kilometers away from Azamgarh city
 lagbhag 15 hajaar kii aabaadi vaala yahi wo gaanv he, jo pichley ek hafte se achaanak hindustan ke nakshe par sabase alag najar aane laga he
 If we believe the claims of the Delhi and Mumbai Police, then most of the boys who have been involved in all the blasts in the country in recent years, belong to this single village
 jishaan, sajid, khalid, saaqib, mohammad sajid, mohammad sadik shaikh, mohammad aarif shaikh, mohammad jakir shaikh, mohammad ansaar shaikh, aftab osmani

 aatif jise police in tamaam ladakon kaa bos bataa rahi he, wo bhi pehle isi sanjarpur gaanv main rahata tha

 jis abu bashar ko gujarat dhamaakon kaa mastermind bataaya ja rahaa he, wo bhi isi gaanv ke thik baraabar ke gaanv binaa paara kaa rahane vaala he

 ek abu bashar ko chhod den, to baaki ke tamaam ladakon ne isi inter college se padhai puri kii he

 ab sawaal ye uthta he ki aakhir ek sampann or khushhaal gaanv ke itane saare ladke bhatak kaise gaye? to isaki do tasviren hai

 is gaanv ke kisi bhi maa-baap se gum-ghumkar puch lijie

 par tasviir kaa ek doosraa pahalu bhi he

 He was the senior of all these boys in school and inter college

 In his first reaction to this decision, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh said, "the time has come for major economic reforms
 " The government has also taken into consideration the opinion of opponents in its decision and empowered the state governments to take a decision on allowing multi-brand retail on their land
 centre sarkaar ke is faisle par charchaa ke liye trinmul ne 18 sitambar ko party sansadeey dal kii baithak bulaai he jisamen party adhyaksh or pashchim bengal kii mukhyamantri mamata banerjee bhaag lengi
 Party MP Kunal Ghosh said in Kolkata, “we have called an urgent meeting of the party parliamentary party on 18 September
 ham in faislon se sahamat nahin hai
 We are giving a last chance of 72 hours, Congress should think again on its decisions
 " unhone kaha, "ham kisi bhi tarah kaa faisla lene ke liye maansik rup se taiyaar hai
 It will take only a second for the Trinamool to withdraw its support from the Center, but if we do, some people will say that we have created the abyss and then the horse-trading of mps will begin
 " Earlier, party leader and Union Minister of State for Health Sudip Bandyopadhyay said, "the decision is unexpected
 ham faisle kaa virodh karenge
 We will discuss this issue within the party
 " It is noteworthy that Left parties including Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP), Samajwadi Party (SP), Trinamool Congress are also strongly opposing it
 kai rajya sarkarein bhi iskaa virodh kar rahi hai
 Anand Sharma said that state governments like Andhra Pradesh, Haryana, Delhi and Maharashtra were in favor of FDI
 unhone kaha, odisha, bihar or pashchim bengal ne iskaa virodh kiya tha
 The comments sharma ne kaha, "jo rajya epadiai chaahate hai, ve aisa kar sakate hai
 States that do not want it can be banned
 " Sharma said that the Department of Industrial Policy and Promotion would soon issue a notification regarding the implementation of the cabinet decision
 unhone kaha, "yah nitigat faisla he
 The department will notify it
 main aapako bharosa dilaataa hum ki is par koi deree nahin hogi
 " aarthik maamalon kii mantrimandaleey samiti kii baithak main shuukravaar ko yah faisla liya gaya
 This decision will allow global retail companies like Walmart and Carefor to open their stores in India
 kai vaishvik companiyon ke bharat main pehle se store hai, lekin unhen sidhe aam logon ko utpaada bechney kaa adhikaar ab tak nahin tha
 They could sell goods to other stores
 ab ve aam logon ko bhi maal bech paaenge
 Information and Broadcasting Minister Ambika Soni and Union Commerce and Industry Minister Anand Sharma announced the decisions taken at a meeting of the Cabinet Committee on Economic Affairs at a joint press conference
 sharma ne bataaya ki ekal brands retail main 100 fisadi or bahubrands retail main 51 fisadi epadiai ko manjuuri di gai he

 " sarkaar ne apane faisle main virodhiyon kii raay ko bhi dhyaan main rakhaa he or rajya sarkaron ko adhikaar diya he ki ve apni bhoomi par bahubrands retail ko anumati dene ke bare main faisla le sakate hai
 On September 18, the Trinamool has called a meeting of the party parliamentary party to discuss the central government's decision in which party president and West Bengal Chief Minister Mamata Banerjee will participate
 party ke saansad kunal ghosh ne kolkata main kaha, "hamane 18 sitambar ko party sansadeey dal kii atyaavashyak baithak bulaai he

 We will oppose the verdict
 is masale par ham party ke andar charchaa karenge

 " Prime Minister Narendra Modi met his Mauritian counterpart Pravind Jaganath on Saturday
 donon ke bich pratinidhamandaleey str kii vaarta hogi
 Foreign Ministry spokesman Gopal Bagle tweeted, "old relations guided by deep friendship and mutual respect
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne hyderabad house main pravind kumaar jagannath se mulaakaat kii
 "after the joint talks, Narendra Modi said that we are happy that the new Prime Minister of Mauritius chose India as his first foreign visit
 hamaare bich do sadiyon kaa gaharaa sambandh he
 He also mentioned his visit to Mauritius 2015
 narendra modi ne kaha ki hind mahaasaagar ke front deshon ke rup main saamudrik suraksha or aarthik gatividhiyon kii suraksha sunishchit karnaa hamaari javabdehi he
 There are challenges like pie racy, drug smuggling, illegal fishing in the Indian Ocean
